### CMD fw4 print

[!] Automatically including '/usr/share/lime/lime-proto-anygw_anycast-rules.nft'
table inet fw4
flush table inet fw4

table inet fw4 {
	#
	# Defines
	#

	define lan_devices = { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" }
	define lan_subnets = { 10.130.0.0/16, fd82:97e1:9645::/64, 10.130.39.194 }

	define wan_devices = { "eth0.1" }
	define wan_subnets = {  }


	#
	# User includes
	#

	include "/etc/nftables.d/*.nft"


	#
	# Filter rules
	#

	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy accept;

		iif "lo" accept comment "!fw4: Accept traffic from loopback"

		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle inbound flows"
		tcp flags & (fin | syn | rst | ack) == syn jump syn_flood comment "!fw4: Rate limit TCP syn packets"
		iifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } jump input_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 input traffic"
		iifname "eth0.1" jump input_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 input traffic"
	}

	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter; policy accept;

		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle forwarded flows"
		iifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } jump forward_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 forward traffic"
		iifname "eth0.1" jump forward_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 forward traffic"
	}

	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy accept;

		oif "lo" accept comment "!fw4: Accept traffic towards loopback"

		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle outbound flows"
		oifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } jump output_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 output traffic"
		oifname "eth0.1" jump output_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 output traffic"
	}

	chain prerouting {
		type filter hook prerouting priority filter; policy accept;
		iifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } jump helper_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 helper assignment"
	}

	chain handle_reject {
		meta l4proto tcp reject with tcp reset comment "!fw4: Reject TCP traffic"
		reject with icmpx type port-unreachable comment "!fw4: Reject any other traffic"
	}

	chain syn_flood {
		limit rate 25/second burst 50 packets return comment "!fw4: Accept SYN packets below rate-limit"
		drop comment "!fw4: Drop excess packets"
	}

	chain input_lan {
		jump accept_from_lan
	}

	chain output_lan {
		jump accept_to_lan
	}

	chain forward_lan {
		jump accept_to_wan comment "!fw4: Accept lan to wan forwarding"
		jump accept_to_lan
	}

	chain helper_lan {
	}

	chain accept_from_lan {
		iifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } counter accept comment "!fw4: accept lan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}

	chain accept_to_lan {
		oifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } counter accept comment "!fw4: accept lan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}

	chain input_wan {
		meta nfproto ipv4 udp dport 68 counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-DHCP-Renew"
		meta nfproto ipv4 icmp type 8 counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-Ping"
		meta nfproto ipv4 meta l4proto igmp counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-IGMP"
		meta nfproto ipv6 udp dport 546 counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-DHCPv6"
		ip6 saddr fe80::/10 icmpv6 type . icmpv6 code { 130 . 0, 131 . 0, 132 . 0, 143 . 0 } counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-MLD"
		meta nfproto ipv6 icmpv6 type { 128, 129, 1, 3, 133, 134 } limit rate 1000/second counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-ICMPv6-Input"
		meta nfproto ipv6 icmpv6 type . icmpv6 code { 2 . 0, 4 . 0, 4 . 1, 135 . 0, 136 . 0 } limit rate 1000/second counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-ICMPv6-Input"
		meta l4proto tcp ip6 saddr fe80::/10 ip6 daddr fe80::/10 counter accept comment "!fw4: lime_allow_wan_all_link_local"
		meta l4proto udp ip6 saddr fe80::/10 ip6 daddr fe80::/10 counter accept comment "!fw4: lime_allow_wan_all_link_local"
		jump reject_from_wan
	}

	chain output_wan {
		jump accept_to_wan
	}

	chain forward_wan {
		meta nfproto ipv6 icmpv6 type { 128, 129, 1, 3 } limit rate 1000/second counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-ICMPv6-Forward"
		meta nfproto ipv6 icmpv6 type . icmpv6 code { 2 . 0, 4 . 0, 4 . 1 } limit rate 1000/second counter accept comment "!fw4: Allow-ICMPv6-Forward"
		meta l4proto esp counter jump accept_to_lan comment "!fw4: Allow-IPSec-ESP"
		udp dport 500 counter jump accept_to_lan comment "!fw4: Allow-ISAKMP"
		jump reject_to_wan
	}

	chain accept_to_wan {
		meta nfproto ipv4 oifname "eth0.1" ct state invalid counter drop comment "!fw4: Prevent NAT leakage"
		oifname "eth0.1" counter accept comment "!fw4: accept wan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}

	chain reject_from_wan {
		iifname "eth0.1" counter jump handle_reject comment "!fw4: reject wan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}

	chain reject_to_wan {
		oifname "eth0.1" counter jump handle_reject comment "!fw4: reject wan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}


	#
	# NAT rules
	#

	chain dstnat {
		type nat hook prerouting priority dstnat; policy accept;
	}

	chain srcnat {
		type nat hook postrouting priority srcnat; policy accept;
		oifname "eth0.1" jump srcnat_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 srcnat traffic"
	}

	chain srcnat_wan {
		meta nfproto ipv4 masquerade comment "!fw4: Masquerade IPv4 wan traffic"
	}


	#
	# Raw rules (notrack)
	#

	chain raw_prerouting {
		type filter hook prerouting priority raw; policy accept;
	}

	chain raw_output {
		type filter hook output priority raw; policy accept;
	}


	#
	# Mangle rules
	#

	chain mangle_prerouting {
		type filter hook prerouting priority mangle; policy accept;
	}

	chain mangle_postrouting {
		type filter hook postrouting priority mangle; policy accept;
		oifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } tcp flags syn / syn,fin,rst tcp option maxseg size set rt mtu comment "!fw4: Zone lan IPv4/IPv6 egress MTU fixing"
		oifname "eth0.1" tcp flags syn / syn,fin,rst tcp option maxseg size set rt mtu comment "!fw4: Zone wan IPv4/IPv6 egress MTU fixing"
	}

	chain mangle_input {
		type filter hook input priority mangle; policy accept;
	}

	chain mangle_output {
		type route hook output priority mangle; policy accept;
	}

	chain mangle_forward {
		type filter hook forward priority mangle; policy accept;
		iifname { "br-lan", "anygw", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17" } tcp flags syn / syn,fin,rst tcp option maxseg size set rt mtu comment "!fw4: Zone lan IPv4/IPv6 ingress MTU fixing"
		iifname "eth0.1" tcp flags syn / syn,fin,rst tcp option maxseg size set rt mtu comment "!fw4: Zone wan IPv4/IPv6 ingress MTU fixing"
	}
}

include "/usr/share/lime/lime-proto-anygw_anycast-rules.nft"

### CMD nft list ruleset

table inet fw4 {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy accept;
		iif "lo" accept comment "!fw4: Accept traffic from loopback"
		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle inbound flows"
		tcp flags & (fin | syn | rst | ack) == syn jump syn_flood comment "!fw4: Rate limit TCP syn packets"
		iifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } jump input_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 input traffic"
		iifname "eth0.1" jump input_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 input traffic"
	}

	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter; policy accept;
		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle forwarded flows"
		iifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } jump forward_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 forward traffic"
		iifname "eth0.1" jump forward_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 forward traffic"
	}

	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy accept;
		oif "lo" accept comment "!fw4: Accept traffic towards loopback"
		ct state vmap { established : accept, related : accept } comment "!fw4: Handle outbound flows"
		oifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } jump output_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 output traffic"
		oifname "eth0.1" jump output_wan comment "!fw4: Handle wan IPv4/IPv6 output traffic"
	}

	chain prerouting {
		type filter hook prerouting priority filter; policy accept;
		iifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } jump helper_lan comment "!fw4: Handle lan IPv4/IPv6 helper assignment"
	}

	chain handle_reject {
		meta l4proto tcp reject with tcp reset comment "!fw4: Reject TCP traffic"
		reject comment "!fw4: Reject any other traffic"
	}

	chain syn_flood {
		limit rate 25/second burst 50 packets return comment "!fw4: Accept SYN packets below rate-limit"
		drop comment "!fw4: Drop excess packets"
	}

	chain input_lan {
		jump accept_from_lan
	}

	chain output_lan {
		jump accept_to_lan
	}

	chain forward_lan {
		jump accept_to_wan comment "!fw4: Accept lan to wan forwarding"
		jump accept_to_lan
	}

	chain helper_lan {
	}

	chain accept_from_lan {
		iifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } counter packets 377331 bytes 38841819 accept comment "!fw4: accept lan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
	}

	chain accept_to_lan {
		oifname { "anygw", "br-lan", "eth0-1_146", "eth0-1_17", "eth1-2_146", "eth1-2_17", "wlan1-mesh_146", "wlan1-mesh_17" } counter packets 2671640 bytes 951403983 accept comment "!fw4: accept lan IPv4/IPv6 traffic"
